namespace = reform_me_events

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.1
	title = reform_me_events.1.t
	desc = reform_me_events.1.d
	picture = LIBERIUM_VETO_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				10 = { set_country_flag = Cortes_Navy }
				10 = { set_country_flag = Cortes_Trade }
				10 = { set_country_flag = Cortes_Goods }
			}
			random_list = {
				10 = { set_country_flag = Cortes_Manpower }
				10 = { set_country_flag = Cortes_Morale }
				10 = { set_country_flag = Cortes_Discipline }
			}
			random_list = {
				10 = { set_country_flag = Cortes_Piety }
				10 = { set_country_flag = Cortes_Gold }
				10 = { set_country_flag = Cortes_Pope }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.1.a
		
		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = has_country_flag
			Cortes_Navy = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = "Cortes_Navy"
					duration = 3650
				}
				clr_country_flag = Cortes_Navy
			}
			Cortes_Trade = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = "Cortes_Trade"
					duration = 3650
				}
				clr_country_flag = Cortes_Trade
			}
			Cortes_Goods = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = "Cortes_Goods"
					duration = 3650
				}
				clr_country_flag = Cortes_Goods
			}
		}
		add_estate_influence_modifier = {
			estate = estate_burghers
			desc = EST_VAL_BURGHERS_ADVANCES
			influence = 10
			duration = 7300
		}
		add_estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_burghers
			loyalty = 10
		}
		clr_country_flag = Cortes_Manpower
		clr_country_flag = Cortes_Morale
		clr_country_flag = Cortes_Discipline
		clr_country_flag = Cortes_Piety
		clr_country_flag = Cortes_Pope
		clr_country_flag = Cortes_Gold
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.1.b
		
		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = has_country_flag
			Cortes_Manpower = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = "Cortes_Manpower"
					duration = 7300
				}
				clr_country_flag = Cortes_Manpower
			}
			Cortes_Morale = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = "Cortes_Morale"
					duration = 7300
				}
				clr_country_flag = Cortes_Morale
			}
			Cortes_Discipline = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = "Cortes_Discipline"
					duration = 7300
				}
				clr_country_flag = Cortes_Discipline
			}
		}
		add_estate_influence_modifier = {
			estate = estate_nobles
			desc = EST_VAL_NOBILITY_ADVANCES
			influence = 10
			duration = 7300
		}
		add_estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_nobles
			loyalty = 10
		}
		clr_country_flag = Cortes_Trade
		clr_country_flag = Cortes_Navy
		clr_country_flag = Cortes_Goods
		clr_country_flag = Cortes_Piety
		clr_country_flag = Cortes_Pope
		clr_country_flag = Cortes_Gold
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.1.c
		
		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = has_country_flag
			Cortes_Piety = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = "Cortes_Piety"
					duration = 7300
				}
				clr_country_flag = Cortes_Piety
			}
			Cortes_Pope = {
				add_papal_influence = 10
				clr_country_flag = Cortes_Pope
			}
			Cortes_Gold = {
				add_years_of_income = 0.8
				clr_country_flag = Cortes_Gold
			}
		}
		add_estate_influence_modifier = {
			estate = estate_church
			desc = EST_VAL_CHURCH_ADVANCE
			influence = 10
			duration = 7300
		}
		add_estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_church
			loyalty = 10
		}
		clr_country_flag = Cortes_Manpower
		clr_country_flag = Cortes_Morale
		clr_country_flag = Cortes_Discipline
		clr_country_flag = Cortes_Trade
		clr_country_flag = Cortes_Navy
		clr_country_flag = Cortes_Goods
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.2
	title = reform_me_events.2.t
	desc = reform_me_events.2.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = POR
		is_year = 1481
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.2.a
		
		add_navy_tradition = 40
		add_government_reform = kingdom_of_portugal_and_azures
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.3
	title = reform_me_events.3.t
	desc = reform_me_events.3.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	

	trigger = {
		has_reform = unrestricted_diplomacy_reform
		any_country = {
			NOT = {
				has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_unrestricted_diplomacy
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_opinion_modifier = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_unrestricted_diplomacy
					}
				}
			}
			add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_unrestricted_diplomacy }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.3.a
		
	}
}

			}
		}
	}

	}
	
	immediate = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_unrestricted_diplomacy
				}
			}
			remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_unrestricted_diplomacy }
		}
	}

	}
}

	}

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.7
	title = reform_me_events.7.t
	desc = reform_me_events.7.d
	picture = BURGHER_ESTATE_UPSET_eventPicture

	trigger = {
		has_reform = rule_by_consent_reform
		NOT = { has_reform = andrea_doria_constitution_reform }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10950
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.7.a
		
		define_ruler = {
			hide_skills = yes
			dip = 1
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.7.b
		
		capital_scope = {
			spawn_rebels = {
				type = pretender_rebels
				size = 3
				win = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.10
	title = reform_me_events.10.t
	desc = reform_me_events.10.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	

	trigger = {
		has_reform = regents_reform
		any_owned_province = {
			development = 20
			OR = {
				culture = dutch
				culture = flemish
			}
			NOT = {	has_province_modifier = Regent_Investments }
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				development = 20
				OR = {
					culture = dutch
					culture = flemish
				}
				NOT = {	has_province_modifier = Regent_Investments }
            }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "Regent_Investments"
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.10.a
		
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.11
	title = reform_me_events.11.t
	desc = reform_me_events.11.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	

	trigger = {
		has_government_attribute = enables_elective_monarchy
		is_lesser_in_union = no
		NOT = { has_country_flag = royal_diet }
	}

	#mean_time_to_happen = {
	#	days = 30
	#}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = royal_diet
			random_neighbor_country = {
				limit = {
					government = monarchy
				}
				save_event_target_as = noble_candidate
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government_attribute = enables_papal_favor
				}
				random_list = {
					33 = { set_country_flag = candidateA }
					33 = { set_country_flag = candidateB }
					33 = { set_country_flag = candidateC }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "reform_me_events.11.a"	# Maintain Hereditary Rule
		
		trigger = {
			ruler_age = 15
		}
		
		add_legitimacy = 10
		add_prestige = 5
		custom_tooltip = born_to_rule_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = candidateA 
			}
			add_papal_influence = 25
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					religion = catholic
					NOT = { has_cardinal = yes }
				}
				add_cardinal = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = candidateA
			clr_country_flag = candidateB
			clr_country_flag = candidateC
			clr_country_flag = royal_diet
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "reform_me_events.11.b"	# A Pretender
		
		trigger = {
			ruler_age = 15
		}
		
		define_ruler = {
			culture = ROOT
			dynasty = ROOT
			age = 40
			male = yes
			adm = -1
			dip = -1
			mil = -1
			claim = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = candidateB
			}
			add_papal_influence = 25
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					religion = catholic
					NOT = { has_cardinal = yes }
				}
				add_cardinal = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = candidateA
			clr_country_flag = candidateB
			clr_country_flag = candidateC
			clr_country_flag = royal_diet
		}
	}
	
	
	option = {
		name = "reform_me_events.11.c"	# Challenger to the crown
		
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government_attribute = enables_royal_electors }
		}
		
		define_ruler = {
			culture = event_target:noble_candidate
			religion = event_target:noble_candidate
			dynasty = event_target:noble_candidate
			hide_skills = yes
			age = 40
			claim = 75
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = candidateC
			}
			add_papal_influence = 25
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					religion = catholic
					NOT = { has_cardinal = yes }
				}
				add_cardinal = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_heir = yes
			clr_country_flag = candidateA
			clr_country_flag = candidateB
			clr_country_flag = candidateC
			clr_country_flag = royal_diet
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "reform_me_events.11.e"	# Elect a Local Regent
		
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_regency = yes
				NOT = { ruler_age = 15 }
			}
		}

		define_ruler = {
			culture = ROOT
			adm = 2
			dip = 2
			mil = 2
			fixed = yes
			regency = yes
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = candidateA
			clr_country_flag = candidateB
			clr_country_flag = candidateC
			clr_country_flag = royal_diet
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "reform_me_events.11.f"	# A Local Noble
		
		trigger = {
			has_government_attribute = enables_noble_electors 
		}
		
		define_ruler = {
			culture = ROOT
			religion = ROOT
			age = 35
			claim = 75
		}
		add_army_tradition = 10
		add_estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_nobles
			loyalty = 10
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "Noble_Privileges"
			duration = 3650
		}
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_heir = yes
			clr_country_flag = candidateA
			clr_country_flag = candidateB
			clr_country_flag = candidateC
			clr_country_flag = royal_diet
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "reform_me_events.11.g"	# Old Family
		
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_regency = yes
				NOT = { ruler_age = 15 }
			}
		}
		
		define_ruler = {
			dynasty = original_dynasty
			culture = ROOT
			religion = ROOT
			age = 35
			claim = 50
		}
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_heir = yes
			clr_country_flag = candidateA
			clr_country_flag = candidateB
			clr_country_flag = candidateC
			clr_country_flag = royal_diet
		}
	}
	
}

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.12
	title = reform_me_events.12.t
	desc = reform_me_events.12.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	

	trigger = {
		has_government_attribute = enables_independent_nobles
		any_owned_province = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_estate = estate_nobles
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = Feudal_Power }
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_estate = estate_nobles }
					has_province_modifier = Feudal_Power
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_estate = estate_nobles
				NOT = {	has_province_modifier = Feudal_Power }
            }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "Feudal_Power"
				duration = -1
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_estate = estate_nobles }
				has_province_modifier = Feudal_Power
            }
			remove_province_modifier = Feudal_Power
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.12.a
		
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.13
	title = reform_me_events.13.t
	desc = reform_me_events.13.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes

            }
			remove_province_modifier = Feudal_Power
		}
	}

	}
}

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.16
	title = reform_me_events.16.t
	desc = reform_me_events.16.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	

	trigger = {
		has_reform = habsburg_monarchy_reform
		any_subject_country = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					religion = catholic
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = Religious_Domination }
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { religion = catholic }
					has_country_modifier = Religious_Domination
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = catholic
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Religious_Domination }
            }
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "Religious_Domination"
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = catholic }
				has_country_modifier = Religious_Domination
            }
			remove_country_modifier = Religious_Domination
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.16.a
		
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.17
	title = reform_me_events.17.t
	desc = reform_me_events.17.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_reform = habsburg_monarchy_reform }
		has_country_modifier = Religious_Domination
		is_subject = no
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = catholic
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Religious_Domination }
            }
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "Religious_Domination"
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = catholic }
				has_country_modifier = Religious_Domination
            }
			remove_country_modifier = Religious_Domination
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.17.a
		
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.18
	title = reform_me_events.18.t
	desc = reform_me_events.18.d
	picture = FARMING_eventPicture
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_reform = austrian_empire_reform
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7300
			
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			has_reform = decentralize_reform
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_reform = centralize_reform
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.90
			has_reform = letat_cest_moi_reform
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			full_idea_group = religious_ideas
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			full_idea_group = humanist_ideas
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			had_active_policy = {
				policy = cultural_unity
				days = 365
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_territory = no
					NOT = { culture_group = ROOT }
				}
				change_culture = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.18.a
		
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.21
	title = reform_me_events.21.t
	desc = reform_me_events.21.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	

	trigger = {
		has_government_attribute = enables_mountain_towns
		any_owned_province = {
			OR = {
				has_terrain = mountain
				has_terrain = hills
				has_terrain = highlands
			}
			NOT = { has_province_modifier = Mountain_Towns }
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 15
	}
	
	immediate = {
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = mountain
					has_terrain = hills
					has_terrain = highlands
				}
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = Mountain_Towns }
            }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "Mountain_Towns"
				duration = -1
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.21.a
		
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.22
	title = reform_me_events.22.t
	desc = reform_me_events.22.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	

	trigger = {
		has_government_attribute = enables_arabian_horses
		OR = {
			AND = {
				calc_true_if = {
					all_subject_country = {
						OR = {
							primary_culture = bedouin_arabic
							primary_culture = mahri_culture
							primary_culture = hejazi_culture
							primary_culture = omani_culture
							primary_culture = yemeni_culture
							primary_culture = gulf_arabic
							primary_culture = al_iraqiya_arabic
						}
					}
					amount = 1
				}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Arabian_Horses_1 }
			}
			AND = {
				calc_true_if = {
					all_subject_country = {
						OR = {
							primary_culture = bedouin_arabic
							primary_culture = mahri_culture
							primary_culture = hejazi_culture
							primary_culture = omani_culture
							primary_culture = yemeni_culture
							primary_culture = gulf_arabic
							primary_culture = al_iraqiya_arabic
						}
					}
					amount = 2
				}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Arabian_Horses_2 }
			}
			AND = {
				calc_true_if = {
					all_subject_country = {
						OR = {
							primary_culture = bedouin_arabic
							primary_culture = mahri_culture
							primary_culture = hejazi_culture
							primary_culture = omani_culture
							primary_culture = yemeni_culture
							primary_culture = gulf_arabic
							primary_culture = al_iraqiya_arabic
						}
					}
					amount = 3
				}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Arabian_Horses_3 }
			}
			AND = {
				calc_true_if = {
					all_subject_country = {
						OR = {
							primary_culture = bedouin_arabic
							primary_culture = mahri_culture
							primary_culture = hejazi_culture
							primary_culture = omani_culture
							primary_culture = yemeni_culture
							primary_culture = gulf_arabic
							primary_culture = al_iraqiya_arabic
						}
					}
					amount = 4
				}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Arabian_Horses_4 }
			}
			AND = {
				calc_true_if = {

						OR = {
							primary_culture = bedouin_arabic
							primary_culture = mahri_culture
							primary_culture = hejazi_culture
							primary_culture = omani_culture
							primary_culture = yemeni_culture
							primary_culture = gulf_arabic
							primary_culture = al_iraqiya_arabic
						}
					}
					amount = 5
				}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Arabian_Horses_5 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				calc_true_if = {
					all_subject_country = {
						OR = {
							primary_culture = bedouin_arabic
							primary_culture = mahri_culture
							primary_culture = hejazi_culture
							primary_culture = omani_culture
							primary_culture = yemeni_culture
							primary_culture = gulf_arabic
							primary_culture = al_iraqiya_arabic
						}
					}
					amount = 1
				}
				NOT = {
					calc_true_if = {
						all_subject_country = {
							OR = {
							primary_culture = bedouin_arabic
							primary_culture = mahri_culture
							primary_culture = hejazi_culture
							primary_culture = omani_culture
							primary_culture = yemeni_culture
							primary_culture = gulf_arabic
							primary_culture = al_iraqiya_arabic
						}
						}
						amount = 2
					}
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = Arabian_Horses_1
				duration = -1
			}
			remove_country_modifier = Arabian_Horses_2
			remove_country_modifier = Arabian_Horses_3
			remove_country_modifier = Arabian_Horses_4
			remove_country_modifier = Arabian_Horses_5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				calc_true_if = {
					all_subject_country = {
						OR = {
							primary_culture = bedouin_arabic
							primary_culture = mahri_culture

							primary_culture = omani_culture
							primary_culture = yemeni_culture
							primary_culture = gulf_arabic
							primary_culture = al_iraqiya_arabic
						}
					}
					amount = 2
				}
				NOT = {

						all_subject_country = {
							OR = {
							primary_culture = bedouin_arabic
							primary_culture = mahri_culture
							primary_culture = hejazi_culture

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.23
	title = reform_me_events.23.t
	desc = reform_me_events.23.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	

	trigger = {
		has_government_attribute = enables_mercenary_markets
		OR = {
			AND = {
				num_of_merchants = 1
				NOT = { num_of_merchants = 2 }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Mercenary_Markets_1 }
			}
			AND = {
				num_of_merchants = 2
				NOT = { num_of_merchants = 3 }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Mercenary_Markets_2 }
			}
			AND = {
				num_of_merchants = 3
				NOT = { num_of_merchants = 4 }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Mercenary_Markets_3 }
			}
			AND = {
				num_of_merchants = 4
				NOT = { num_of_merchants = 5 }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Mercenary_Markets_4 }
			}
			AND = {
				num_of_merchants = 5
				NOT = { num_of_merchants = 6 }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Mercenary_Markets_5 }
			}
			AND = {
				num_of_merchants = 6
				NOT = { num_of_merchants = 7 }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Mercenary_Markets_6 }
			}
			AND = {
				num_of_merchants = 7
				NOT = { num_of_merchants = 8 }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Mercenary_Markets_7 }
			}
			AND = {
				num_of_merchants = 8
				NOT = { num_of_merchants = 9 }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Mercenary_Markets_8 }
			}
			AND = {
				num_of_merchants = 9
				NOT = { num_of_merchants = 10 }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Mercenary_Markets_9 }
			}
			AND = {
				num_of_merchants = 10
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Mercenary_Markets_10 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {

	}

				duration = -1

			remove_country_modifier = Mercenary_Markets_7

			remove_country_modifier = Mercenary_Markets_10

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.24
	title = reform_me_events.24.t
	desc = reform_me_events.24.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	

	trigger = {
		has_government_attribute = enables_national_strenghtening_project
		any_owned_province = {
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
			NOT = { has_province_modifier = National_Strenghtening_Project }
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = National_Strenghtening_Project }
            }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "National_Strenghtening_Project"
				duration = -1
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_owner_accepted_culture = no
				has_province_modifier = National_Strenghtening_Project
            }
			remove_province_modifier = National_Strenghtening_Project
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.24.a
		
	}
}

	id = reform_me_events.25
	title = reform_me_events.25.t
	desc = reform_me_events.25.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes

		OR = {
			any_owned_province = {
				culture = ROOT
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = Patriotism }
			}
			any_owned_province = {
				NOT = { culture = ROOT }
				has_province_modifier = Patriotism
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {

				culture = ROOT
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = Patriotism }
            }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "Patriotism"
				duration = -1
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { culture = ROOT }
				has_province_modifier = Patriotism
            }
			remove_province_modifier = Patriotism
		}

	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.25.a

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.29
	title = reform_me_events.29.t
	desc = reform_me_events.29.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	

	trigger = { 
		has_government_attribute = enables_administrative_forts 
		any_owned_province = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					any_province_in_state = {
						fort_level = 2
						}
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = "Administrative_Forts" }
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						any_province_in_state = {
							fort_level = 2
						}
					}
					has_province_modifier = Administrative_Forts
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				any_province_in_state = {
					fort_level = 2
					}
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = "Administrative_Forts" }
            }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "Administrative_Forts"
				duration = -1
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_province_in_state = {
						fort_level = 2
					}
				}
				has_province_modifier = Administrative_Forts
            }
			remove_province_modifier = Administrative_Forts
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.29.a
		
	}
}

				num_of_generals = 1
				NOT = { num_of_generals = 2 }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = General_Connections_1 }
			}
			AND = {
				num_of_generals = 2
				NOT = { num_of_generals = 3 }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = General_Connections_2 }
			}
			AND = {
				num_of_generals = 3
				NOT = { num_of_generals = 4 }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = General_Connections_3 }
			}
			AND = {
				num_of_generals = 4
				NOT = { num_of_generals = 5 }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = General_Connections_4 }
			}
			AND = {
				num_of_generals = 5
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = General_Connections_5 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_generals = 1
				NOT = { num_of_generals = 2 }
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "General_Connections_1" 
				duration = -1
			}
			remove_country_modifier = General_Connections_2 
			remove_country_modifier = General_Connections_3 
			remove_country_modifier = General_Connections_4 
			remove_country_modifier = General_Connections_5 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_generals = 2
				NOT = { num_of_generals = 3 }
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "General_Connections_2"
				duration = -1
			}
			remove_country_modifier = General_Connections_1 
			remove_country_modifier = General_Connections_3 
			remove_country_modifier = General_Connections_4 
			remove_country_modifier = General_Connections_5  
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_generals = 3
				NOT = { num_of_generals = 4 }
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "General_Connections_3"
				duration = -1
			}
			remove_country_modifier = General_Connections_1 
			remove_country_modifier = General_Connections_2 
			remove_country_modifier = General_Connections_4 
			remove_country_modifier = General_Connections_5 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_generals = 4
				NOT = { num_of_generals = 5 }
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "General_Connections_4"
				duration = -1
			}
			remove_country_modifier = General_Connections_1 
			remove_country_modifier = General_Connections_2 
			remove_country_modifier = General_Connections_3 
			remove_country_modifier = General_Connections_5 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_generals = 5
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "General_Connections_5"
				duration = -1
			}
			remove_country_modifier = General_Connections_1
			remove_country_modifier = General_Connections_2 
			remove_country_modifier = General_Connections_3 
			remove_country_modifier = General_Connections_4 
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.35.a
		
	}
}

				}
				AND = {

							has_seat_in_parliament = yes
						}
					}
					has_province_modifier = Bureacratic_Apparatus
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				any_province_in_state = {
					has_seat_in_parliament = yes
					}
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = "Bureacratic_Apparatus" }
            }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "Bureacratic_Apparatus"
				duration = -1
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_province_in_state = {
						has_seat_in_parliament = yes
					}
				}
				has_province_modifier = Bureacratic_Apparatus
            }
			remove_province_modifier = Bureacratic_Apparatus
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.39.a
		
	}

			}

				}

				duration = -1

			remove_country_modifier = Pride_of_the_Navy_3 
			remove_country_modifier = Pride_of_the_Navy_4 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				navy_tradition = 40
				NOT = {
					navy_tradition = 60
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = Pride_of_the_Navy_2 
				duration = -1
			}
			remove_country_modifier = Pride_of_the_Navy_1
			remove_country_modifier = Pride_of_the_Navy_3 
			remove_country_modifier = Pride_of_the_Navy_4 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				navy_tradition = 60
				NOT = {
					navy_tradition = 80
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = Pride_of_the_Navy_3 
				duration = -1
			}
			remove_country_modifier = Pride_of_the_Navy_1 
			remove_country_modifier = Pride_of_the_Navy_2 
			remove_country_modifier = Pride_of_the_Navy_4

		set_ruler_flag = council_picked	
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					adm = 5
				}
				random_list = {
					10 = { set_country_flag = Bad_Admin }
					65 = { set_country_flag = Decent_Admin }
					25 = { set_country_flag = Good_Admin }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					adm = 3
				}
				random_list = {
					40 = { set_country_flag = Bad_Admin }
					50 = { set_country_flag = Decent_Admin }
					10 = { set_country_flag = Good_Admin }
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					70 = { set_country_flag = Bad_Admin }
					25 = { set_country_flag = Decent_Admin }
					5 = { set_country_flag = Good_Admin }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					dip = 5
				}
				random_list = {
					10 = { set_country_flag = Bad_Diplo }
					65 = { set_country_flag = Decent_Diplo }
					25 = { set_country_flag = Good_Diplo }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					dip = 3
				}
				random_list = {
					40 = { set_country_flag = Bad_Diplo }
					50 = { set_country_flag = Decent_Diplo }
					10 = { set_country_flag = Good_Diplo }
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					70 = { set_country_flag = Bad_Diplo }
					25 = { set_country_flag = Decent_Diplo }
					5 = { set_country_flag = Good_Diplo }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					mil = 5
				}
				random_list = {
					10 = { set_country_flag = Bad_Mil }
					65 = { set_country_flag = Decent_Mil }
					25 = { set_country_flag = Good_Mil }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					mil = 3
				}
				random_list = {
					40 = { set_country_flag = Bad_Mil }
					50 = { set_country_flag = Decent_Mil }
					10 = { set_country_flag = Good_Mil }
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					70 = { set_country_flag = Bad_Mil }
					25 = { set_country_flag = Decent_Mil }
					5 = { set_country_flag = Good_Mil }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.52.a
		
		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = has_country_flag
			Bad_Admin = {
				add_ruler_modifier = {
					name = "Bad_Admin"
					duration = -1
				}
				clr_country_flag = Bad_Admin
			}
			Decent_Admin = {
				add_ruler_modifier = {
					name = "Decent_Admin"
					duration = -1
				}
				clr_country_flag = Decent_Admin
			}
			Good_Admin = {
				add_ruler_modifier = {
					name = "Good_Admin"
					duration = -1
				}
				clr_country_flag = Good_Admin
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_estate = estate_church
				NOT = { has_reform = states_general_reform }
			}
			add_estate_influence_modifier = {
				estate = estate_church
				desc = EST_VAL_CLERGY_ADVANCES
				influence = 10
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = Bad_Diplo
		clr_country_flag = Decent_Diplo
		clr_country_flag = Good_Diplo
		clr_country_flag = Bad_Mil
		clr_country_flag = Decent_Mil
		clr_country_flag = Good_Mil
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.52.b
		
		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = has_country_flag
			Bad_Diplo = {
				add_ruler_modifier = {
					name = "Bad_Diplo"
					duration = -1
				}
				clr_country_flag = Bad_Diplo
			}
			Decent_Diplo = {

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.53
	title = reform_me_events.53.t
	desc = reform_me_events.53.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	

	trigger = {
		has_government_attribute = enables_morisca_band
		OR = {
			any_owned_province = {
				fort_level = 2
				any_neighbor_province = {
					religion_group = christian
					has_owner_religion = yes
				}
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = Morisca_Band }
			}
			AND = {
				any_owned_province = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { fort_level = 2 }
						NOT = {
							any_neighbor_province = {
								religion_group = christian
								has_owner_religion = yes
							}
						}
					}
					has_province_modifier = Morisca_Band 
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				fort_level = 2
				any_neighbor_province = {
					religion_group = christian
					has_owner_religion = yes
				}
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = Morisca_Band }
            }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "Morisca_Band"
				duration = -1
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { fort_level = 2 }
					NOT = {
						any_neighbor_province = {
							religion_group = christian
							has_owner_religion = yes
						}
					}
				}
				has_province_modifier = Morisca_Band 
			}
			remove_province_modifier = Morisca_Band 
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.53.a
		
	}
}

	title = reform_me_events.62.t
	desc = reform_me_events.62.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	

	trigger = {
		has_government_attribute = enables_trade_princes
		OR = {
			AND = {
				calc_true_if = {
					any_subject_country = {
						OR = {
							primary_culture = aragonese 
							primary_culture = catalan 
							primary_culture = portugese
							primary_culture = andalucian
							primary_culture = basque
							primary_culture = leonese
							primary_culture = asturian
						}
					}
					amount = 1
				}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Trade_Princes }
			}
			NOT = {
				calc_true_if = {
					any_subject_country = {
						OR = {
							primary_culture = aragonese 
							primary_culture = catalan 
							primary_culture = portugese
							primary_culture = andalucian
							primary_culture = basque
							primary_culture = leonese
							primary_culture = asturian
						}
					}
				amount = 1
				}
				has_country_modifier = Trade_Princes
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				calc_true_if = {
					any_subject_country = {
						OR = {
							primary_culture = aragonese 
							primary_culture = catalan 
							primary_culture = portugese
							primary_culture = andalucian
							primary_culture = basque
							primary_culture = leonese
							primary_culture = asturian
						}
					}
					amount = 1
				}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Trade_Princes }
            }
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "Trade_Princes"
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 				
					calc_true_if = {
						all_subject_country = {
							OR = {
								primary_culture = aragonese 
								primary_culture = catalan 
								primary_culture = portugese
								primary_culture = andalucian
								primary_culture = basque
								primary_culture = leonese
								primary_culture = asturian
							}
						}
						amount = 1
					}
				}
			}
			remove_country_modifier = Trade_Princes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.62.a
		
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.70
	title = reform_me_events.70.t
	desc = reform_me_events.70.d
	picture = FARMING_eventPicture
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_government_attribute = enables_religious_supremacy
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7300
			
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = {
				has_global_modifier_value = {
					which = tolerance_heathen
					value = 1
				} 
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_global_modifier_value = {
				which = tolerance_heathen
				value = 2
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.50
			has_global_modifier_value = {
				which = tolerance_heathen
				value = 3
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			full_idea_group = religious_ideas
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			full_idea_group = humanist_ideas
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_building = temple
					is_territory = no
					NOT = { nationalism = 1 }
					NOT = { religion = ROOT }
				}
				change_religion = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.70.a
		
	}
}

		every_owned_province = {

				NOT = { 
					OR = {
						has_building = temple
						has_building = cathedral
					} 
				}
				has_province_modifier = Church_Poorhouses
            }
			remove_province_modifier = Church_Poorhouses
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.74.a
		
	}
}

	}

			limit = {
				AND = {
					employed_advisor = {
						category = ADM
					}
					employed_advisor = {
						category = DIP
					}
					employed_advisor = {
						category = MIL
					}
				}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = "Peasant_Council" }

			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "Peasant_Council"
				duration = -1
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						employed_advisor = {
							category = ADM
						}
						employed_advisor = {
							category = DIP
						}
						employed_advisor = {
							category = MIL
						}
					}
				}
				has_country_modifier = "Peasant_Council"
			}
			remove_country_modifier = Peasant_Council
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.91.a

				}
				has_country_modifier = Recognize_No_Crown
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 15
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_ally = {
					NOT = {
						government = monarchy
					}
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "Recognize_No_Crown"
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_ally = {
					government = monarchy
				}
			}
			remove_country_modifier = Recognize_No_Crown
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.9100.a
		
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.100
	title = reform_me_events.100.t
	desc = reform_me_events.100.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	

	trigger = {
		has_government_attribute = enables_attracting_academics
		OR = {
			AND = {
				prestige = 20
				NOT = {
					prestige = 40
				}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Hansa_Academics_1 }
			}
			AND = {
				prestige = 40
				NOT = {
					prestige = 60
				}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Hansa_Academics_2 }
			}
			AND = {
				prestige = 60
				NOT = {
					prestige = 80
				}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Hansa_Academics_3 }
			}
			AND = {
				prestige = 80
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Hansa_Academics_4 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				prestige = 20
				NOT = {
					prestige = 40
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = Hansa_Academics_1 
				duration = -1
			}
			remove_country_modifier = Hansa_Academics_2 
			remove_country_modifier = Hansa_Academics_3 
			remove_country_modifier = Hansa_Academics_4 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				prestige = 40
				NOT = {
					prestige = 60
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = Hansa_Academics_2 
				duration = -1
			}
			remove_country_modifier = Hansa_Academics_1
			remove_country_modifier = Hansa_Academics_3 
			remove_country_modifier = Hansa_Academics_4 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				prestige = 60
				NOT = {
					prestige = 80
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = Hansa_Academics_3 
				duration = -1
			}
			remove_country_modifier = Hansa_Academics_1 
			remove_country_modifier = Hansa_Academics_2 
			remove_country_modifier = Hansa_Academics_4 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				prestige = 80
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = Hansa_Academics_4
				duration = -1
			}
			remove_country_modifier = Hansa_Academics_1 
			remove_country_modifier = Hansa_Academics_2 
			remove_country_modifier = Hansa_Academics_3 
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.44.a
		
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.115
	title = reform_me_events.115.t
	desc = reform_me_events.115.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	

	trigger = {
		has_government_attribute = enables_lingua_franca
		OR = {
			any_country = {
				OR = {
					marriage_with = ROOT
					alliance_with = ROOT
					guaranteed_by = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					has_opinion_modifier = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_lingua_franca
					}
				}
			}
			any_country = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						marriage_with = ROOT
						alliance_with = ROOT
						guaranteed_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_lingua_franca
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					marriage_with = ROOT
					alliance_with = ROOT
					guaranteed_by = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					has_opinion_modifier = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_lingua_franca
					}
				}
			}
			add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_lingua_franca }
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						marriage_with = ROOT
						alliance_with = ROOT
						guaranteed_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_lingua_franca
				}
			}
			remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_lingua_franca }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.115.a
		
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.117
	title = reform_me_events.117.t
	desc = reform_me_events.117.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	

	trigger = {
		has_government_attribute = enables_industrialism 
		any_owned_province = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						has_building = workshop
					}
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = Promoted_Industry }
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						has_building = counting_house 
					}
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = Promoted_Industry_v2 }
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						has_building = steam_factory 
					}
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = Promoted_Industry_v3 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_building = workshop 
				}
				NOT = {	has_province_modifier = Promoted_Industry }
            }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "Promoted_Industry"
				duration = -1
				hidden = yes
			}
			#remove_province_modifier = Promoted_Industry
			remove_province_modifier = Promoted_Industry_v2
			remove_province_modifier = Promoted_Industry_v3
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_building = counting_house 
				}
				NOT = {	has_province_modifier = Promoted_Industry_v2 }
            }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "Promoted_Industry_v2"
				duration = -1
				hidden = yes
			}
			remove_province_modifier = Promoted_Industry
			#remove_province_modifier = Promoted_Industry_v2
			remove_province_modifier = Promoted_Industry_v3
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_building = steam_factory
				}
				NOT = {	has_province_modifier = Promoted_Industry_v3 }
            }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "Promoted_Industry_v3"
				duration = -1
				hidden = yes
			}
			remove_province_modifier = Promoted_Industry
			remove_province_modifier = Promoted_Industry_v2
			#remove_province_modifier = Promoted_Industry_v3
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.117.a
		
	}
}

country_event = {

	title = reform_me_events.118.t
	desc = reform_me_events.118.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	

	trigger = {
		has_government_attribute = enables_home_market
		OR = {
			AND = {

				NOT = { mercantilism = 20 }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Home_Market_1 }
			}
			AND = {

				mercantilism = 60
				NOT = { mercantilism = 70 }

				NOT = { mercantilism = 80 }

			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_10

				duration = -1

			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_3
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_4
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_5
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_6

			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_6
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_7
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_8

		}

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.121
	title = reform_me_events.121.t
	desc = reform_me_events.121.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	

	trigger = {
		has_government_attribute = enables_economic_block 
		OR = {
			AND = {
				num_of_allies = 1
				NOT = { num_of_allies = 2 }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Home_Market_1 }
			}
			AND = {
				num_of_allies = 2
				NOT = { num_of_allies = 3 }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Home_Market_2 }
			}
			AND = {
				num_of_allies = 3
				NOT = { num_of_allies = 4 }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Home_Market_3 }
			}
			AND = {
				num_of_allies = 4
				NOT = { num_of_allies = 5 }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Home_Market_4 }
			}
			AND = {
				num_of_allies = 5
				NOT = { num_of_allies = 6 }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Home_Market_5 }
			}
			AND = {
				num_of_allies = 6
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Home_Market_6 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_allies = 0
				NOT = { num_of_allies = 1 }
			}
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_1
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_2
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_3
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_4
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_5
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_6
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_allies = 1
				NOT = { num_of_allies = 2 }
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = Home_Market_1
				duration = -1
			}
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_2
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_3
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_4
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_5
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_6
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_allies = 2
				NOT = { num_of_allies = 3 }
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = Home_Market_2
				duration = -1
			}
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_1
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_3
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_4
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_5
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_6
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_allies = 3
				NOT = { num_of_allies = 4 }
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = Home_Market_3
				duration = -1
			}
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_1
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_2
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_4
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_5
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_6
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_allies = 4
				NOT = { num_of_allies = 5 }
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = Home_Market_4
				duration = -1
			}
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_1
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_2
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_3
			remove_country_modifier = Home_Market_5

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.135
	title = reform_me_events.135.t
	desc = reform_me_events.135.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	

	trigger = {
		has_government_attribute = enables_hansa_ties
		OR = {
			AND = {
				calc_true_if = {
					all_country = {
						government = republic
						OR = {
							is_subject_of = ROOT
							alliance_with = ROOT
						}
					}
					amount = 1
				}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Hansa_Ties_1 }
			}
			AND = {
				calc_true_if = {
					all_country = {
						government = republic
						OR = {
							is_subject_of = ROOT
							alliance_with = ROOT
						}
					}
					amount = 2
				}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Hansa_Ties_2 }
			}
			AND = {
				calc_true_if = {
					all_country = {
						government = republic
						OR = {
							is_subject_of = ROOT
							alliance_with = ROOT
						}
					}
					amount = 3
				}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Hansa_Ties_3 }
			}
			AND = {
				calc_true_if = {
					all_country = {
						government = republic
						OR = {
							is_subject_of = ROOT
							alliance_with = ROOT
						}
					}
					amount = 4
				}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Hansa_Ties_4 }
			}
			AND = {
				calc_true_if = {
					all_country = {
						government = republic
						OR = {
							is_subject_of = ROOT
							alliance_with = ROOT
						}
					}
					amount = 5
				}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Hansa_Ties_5 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				calc_true_if = {
					all_country = {
						government = republic
						OR = {
							is_subject_of = ROOT
							alliance_with = ROOT
						}
					}
					amount = 1
				}
				NOT = {
					calc_true_if = {
						all_country = {
							government = republic
							OR = {
								is_subject_of = ROOT
								alliance_with = ROOT
							}
						}
						amount = 2
					}
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = Hansa_Ties_1
				duration = -1
			}
			remove_country_modifier = Hansa_Ties_2
			remove_country_modifier = Hansa_Ties_3
			remove_country_modifier = Hansa_Ties_4
			remove_country_modifier = Hansa_Ties_5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				calc_true_if = {
					all_country = {
						government = republic
						OR = {
							is_subject_of = ROOT
							alliance_with = ROOT
						}
					}
					amount = 2
				}
				NOT = { 				
					calc_true_if = {
						all_country = {
							government = republic
							OR = {
								is_subject_of = ROOT
								alliance_with = ROOT
							}
						}
						amount = 3
					}
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = Hansa_Ties_2
				duration = -1
			}
			remove_country_modifier = Hansa_Ties_1
			remove_country_modifier = Hansa_Ties_3
			remove_country_modifier = Hansa_Ties_4
			remove_country_modifier = Hansa_Ties_5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				calc_true_if = {
					all_country = {

						OR = {
							is_subject_of = ROOT
							alliance_with = ROOT
						}
					}
					amount = 3
				}
				NOT = { 				
					calc_true_if = {
						all_country = {
							government = republic
							OR = {
								is_subject_of = ROOT
								alliance_with = ROOT
							}
						}
						amount = 4
					}
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = Hansa_Ties_3
				duration = -1
			}
			remove_country_modifier = Hansa_Ties_1
			remove_country_modifier = Hansa_Ties_2
			remove_country_modifier = Hansa_Ties_4
			remove_country_modifier = Hansa_Ties_5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				calc_true_if = {
					all_country = {
						government = republic
						OR = {
							is_subject_of = ROOT
							alliance_with = ROOT
						}
					}
					amount = 4
				}

							government = republic
							OR = {

						}

			}

				duration = -1

			remove_country_modifier = Hansa_Ties_1
			remove_country_modifier = Hansa_Ties_2
			remove_country_modifier = Hansa_Ties_3
			remove_country_modifier = Hansa_Ties_5

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.141
	title = reform_me_events.141.t
	desc = reform_me_events.141.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	

	trigger = {
		has_government_attribute = enables_royal_army_garrisons
		any_owned_province = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							has_estate = estate_burghers
							has_estate = estate_church
							has_estate = estate_nobles
						}
					}
					is_territory = no
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = Royal_Army_Garrison }
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						has_estate = estate_burghers
						has_estate = estate_church
						has_estate = estate_nobles
					}
					has_province_modifier = Royal_Army_Garrison
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_estate = estate_burghers
						has_estate = estate_church
						has_estate = estate_nobles
					}
				}
				is_territory = no
				NOT = {	has_province_modifier = Royal_Army_Garrison }
            }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "Royal_Army_Garrison"
				duration = -1
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_estate = estate_burghers
					has_estate = estate_church
					has_estate = estate_nobles
				}
				has_province_modifier = Royal_Army_Garrison
            }
			remove_province_modifier = Royal_Army_Garrison
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.141.a
		
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.150
	title = reform_me_events.150.t
	desc = reform_me_events.150.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_government_attribute = enables_custodian_of_cities
				OR = {
					AND = {
						owns = 384
						owns = 385
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = GE_Good_Custodian }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { 
							owns = 384
							owns = 385 
						}
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = GE_Bad_Custodian }
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_country_modifier = GE_Bad_Custodian
					has_country_modifier = GE_Good_Custodian
				}
				NOT = { has_government_attribute = enables_custodian_of_cities }
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.150.a
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns = 384
				owns = 385
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = GE_Good_Custodian }
			}
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Bad_Custodian
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = GE_Good_Custodian
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					owns = 384
					owns = 385 
				}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = GE_Bad_Custodian }
			}
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Good_Custodian
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = GE_Bad_Custodian
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_modifier = GE_Bad_Custodian
					has_country_modifier = GE_Good_Custodian
				}
				NOT = { has_government_attribute = enables_custodian_of_cities }
			}
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Good_Custodian
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Bad_Custodian
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.152
	title = reform_me_events.152.t
	desc = reform_me_events.152.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_government_attribute = enables_qadi_authority
				any_owned_province = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							has_owner_religion = yes
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = GE_Qadi_Authority }
						}
						AND = {
							NOT = { has_owner_religion = yes }
							has_province_modifier = GE_Qadi_Authority
						}
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { has_government_attribute = enables_qadi_authority }
				any_owned_province = {
					has_province_modifier = GE_Qadi_Authority
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.152.a
		
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_owner_religion = yes
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = GE_Qadi_Authority }
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = GE_Qadi_Authority
				duration = -1
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_owner_religion = yes }
				has_province_modifier = GE_Qadi_Authority
			}
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Qadi_Authority
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				owner = {NOT = { has_government_attribute = enables_qadi_authority }}
			}
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Qadi_Authority
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.15200
	title = reform_me_events.15200.t
	desc = reform_me_events.15200.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_government_attribute = enables_millet_system
				any_owned_province = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							OR = {
								has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
								has_owner_culture = yes
							}
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = GE_Millet_System }
						}
						AND = {
							OR = {
								has_owner_accepted_culture = no
								has_owner_culture = no
							}
							has_province_modifier = GE_Millet_System
						}
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { has_government_attribute = enables_millet_system }
				any_owned_province = {
					has_province_modifier = GE_Millet_System
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.15200.a
		
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = GE_Millet_System }
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = GE_Millet_System
				duration = -1
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_owner_accepted_culture = no
				}
				has_province_modifier = GE_Millet_System
			}
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Millet_System
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				owner = {NOT = { has_government_attribute = enables_millet_system }}
			}
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Millet_System
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_government_attribute = enables_janissary_guards
				OR = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { janissary_percentage = 0.2 }
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = GE_Janissary_Guards }
					}
					AND = {
						janissary_percentage = 0.2
						has_country_modifier = GE_Janissary_Guards
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { has_government_attribute = enables_janissary_guards }
				has_country_modifier = GE_Janissary_Guards
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.155.a
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { janissary_percentage = 0.2 }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = GE_Janissary_Guards }
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = GE_Janissary_Guards
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				janissary_percentage = 0.2
				has_country_modifier = GE_Janissary_Guards
			}
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Janissary_Guards
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_government_attribute = enables_janissary_guards }
			}
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Janissary_Guards
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.156
	title = reform_me_events.156.t
	desc = reform_me_events.156.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture

	trigger = {
		has_government_attribute = enables_koprulu_dynasty
		OR = {
			had_country_flag = {
				flag = GE_Koprulu_Dynasty_Flag
				days = 9125
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GE_Koprulu_Dynasty_Flag }
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = GE_Koprulu_Dynasty_Flag
			set_country_flag = GE_Koprulu_Dynasty_Flag
			every_owned_province = {
				remove_province_modifier = GE_Koprulu_Defence_Local
				remove_province_modifier = GE_Koprulu_Economy_Local
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.156.a
		
		custom_tooltip = GE_Koprulu_Defence_Event
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					any_neighbor_province = {
						NOT = {
							owned_by = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = GE_Koprulu_Defence_Local #15% Fort Defence
					duration = 9125
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.156.b
		
		custom_tooltip = GE_Koprulu_Economy_Event
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = grain
						trade_goods = livestock
					}
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = GE_Koprulu_Economy_Local #10% Goods Produced
					duration = 9125
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.156.c
		
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = GE_Koprulu_Court #-0.05 Corruption
			duration = 9125
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.157
	title = reform_me_events.157.t
	desc = reform_me_events.157.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_government_attribute = enables_public_works
				any_owned_province = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							OR = {
								has_building = courthouse
								has_building = town_hall
								has_building = government_lvl_3
								has_building = government_lvl_4
							}
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = GE_Public_Works }
						}
						AND = {
							NOT = { 
								OR = {
									has_building = courthouse
									has_building = town_hall
									has_building = government_lvl_3
									has_building = government_lvl_4
								}
							}
							has_province_modifier = GE_Public_Works
						}
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { has_government_attribute = enables_public_works }
				any_owned_province = {
					has_province_modifier = GE_Public_Works
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.157.a
		
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_building = courthouse
					has_building = town_hall
					has_building = government_lvl_3
					has_building = government_lvl_4
				}
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = GE_Public_Works }
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = GE_Public_Works
				duration = -1
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					OR = {
						has_building = courthouse
						has_building = town_hall
						has_building = government_lvl_3
						has_building = government_lvl_4
					}
				}
				has_province_modifier = GE_Public_Works
			}
			remove_province_modifier = GE_Public_Works
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_government_attribute = enables_public_works }
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				remove_province_modifier = GE_Public_Works
			}
		}
	}
}

				AND = {
					has_estate = estate_rajput
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = GE_Rajput_Law }
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_estate = estate_rajput }
					has_province_modifier = GE_Rajput_Law
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_estate = estate_rajput
				NOT = {	has_province_modifier = GE_Rajput_Law }
            }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "GE_Rajput_Law"
				duration = -1
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_estate = estate_rajput }
				has_province_modifier = GE_Rajput_Law
            }
			remove_province_modifier = GE_Rajput_Law
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.160.a
		
	}
}

						accepted_culture = bornean

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.165
	title = reform_me_events.165.t
	desc = reform_me_events.165.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture

	trigger = {
		has_government_attribute = enables_roman_empire
		OR = {
			had_country_flag = {
				flag = GE_Roman_Empire_Flag
				days = 9125
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GE_Roman_Empire_Flag }
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = GE_Roman_Empire_Flag
			set_country_flag = GE_Roman_Empire_Flag
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.165.a
		
		change_adm = 1
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = GE_Roman_Empire_Administration #-15% State Maintenance
			duration = 9125
		}
		add_faction_influence = {
			faction = GE_Senate
			influence = 25
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.165.b
		
		change_dip = 1
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = GE_Roman_Empire_Corruption #-0.05 Corruption
			duration = 9125
		}
		add_faction_influence = {
			faction = GE_Pentarchy
			influence = 25
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.165.c
		
		change_mil = 1
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = GE_Roman_Empire_Drill #25% Drill
			duration = 9125
		}
		add_faction_influence = {
			faction = GE_Army
			influence = 25
		}
	}
}


country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.166
	title = reform_me_events.166.t
	desc = reform_me_events.166.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	

	trigger = { 
		has_government_attribute = enables_fortified_settlements 
		any_owned_province = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					any_province_in_state = {
						fort_level = 2
						}
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = "GE_Fortified_Settlement" }
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						any_province_in_state = {
							fort_level = 2
						}
					}
					has_province_modifier = GE_Fortified_Settlement
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				any_province_in_state = {
					fort_level = 2
					}
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = "GE_Fortified_Settlement" }
            }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = "GE_Fortified_Settlement"
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_province_in_state = {
						fort_level = 2
					}
				}
				has_province_modifier = GE_Fortified_Settlement
            }
			remove_province_modifier = GE_Fortified_Settlement
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.166.a
		
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.169
	title = reform_me_events.169.t
	desc = reform_me_events.169.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	

	trigger = {
		has_government_attribute = enables_varangian_guard 
		OR = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					any_ally = {
						culture_group = scandinavian 
					}
					any_subject_country = {
						culture_group = scandinavian
					}
				}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = GE_Varangian_Guard }
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { 
					OR = {
						any_ally = {
							culture_group = scandinavian
						}
						any_subject_country = {
							culture_group = scandinavian
						}
					} 
				}
				has_country_modifier = GE_Varangian_Guard
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					any_ally = {
						culture_group = scandinavian
					}
					any_subject_country = {
						culture_group = scandinavian
					}
				}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = GE_Varangian_Guard }
            }
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "GE_Varangian_Guard"
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					OR = {
						any_ally = {
							culture_group = scandinavian
						}
						any_subject_country = {
							culture_group = scandinavian
						}
					} 
				}
				has_country_modifier = GE_Varangian_Guard
            }
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Varangian_Guard
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.169.a
		
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.173
	title = reform_me_events.168.t
	desc = reform_me_events.168.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	

	trigger = {
		has_government_attribute = enables_peace_development_reduction 
		OR = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					is_at_war = yes
					had_recent_war = 10
				}
				OR = {
					has_country_modifier = Hermit_five
					has_country_modifier = Hermit_ten
					has_country_modifier = Hermit_fifteen
				}
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Hermit_five }
				NOT = { had_recent_war = 10 }
				had_recent_war = 15
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Hermit_ten }
				NOT = { had_recent_war = 15 }
				had_recent_war = 20
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Hermit_fifteen }
				NOT = { had_recent_war = 20 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		remove_country_modifier = Hermit_five
		remove_country_modifier = Hermit_ten
		remove_country_modifier = Hermit_fifteen
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Hermit_five }
				NOT = { had_recent_war = 10 }
				NOT = { is_at_war = yes }
				had_recent_war = 15
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = Hermit_five
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Hermit_ten }
				NOT = { had_recent_war = 15 }
				NOT = { is_at_war = yes }
				had_recent_war = 20
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = Hermit_ten
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_at_war = yes }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = Hermit_five }
				NOT = { had_recent_war = 20 }
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = Hermit_fifteen
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.168.a
		
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.183
	title = reform_me_events.183.t
	desc = reform_me_events.183.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		has_government_attribute = enables_elephant_cavalry
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_global_modifier_value = {
					which = cavalry_power
					value = 0.05
				}
				NOT = {
					has_global_modifier_value = {
						which = cavalry_power
						value = 0.10
					}
				}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_1 }
			}
			AND = {
				has_global_modifier_value = {
					which = cavalry_power
					value = 0.10
				}
				NOT = {
					has_global_modifier_value = {
						which = cavalry_power
						value = 0.15
					}
				}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_2 }
			}
			AND = {
				has_global_modifier_value = {
					which = cavalry_power
					value = 0.15
				}
				NOT = {
					has_global_modifier_value = {
						which = cavalry_power
						value = 0.20
					}
				}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_3 }
			}
			AND = {
				has_global_modifier_value = {
					which = cavalry_power
					value = 0.20
				}
				NOT = {
					has_global_modifier_value = {
						which = cavalry_power
						value = 0.25
					}
				}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_4 }
			}
			AND = {
				has_global_modifier_value = {
					which = cavalry_power
					value = 0.25
				}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_5 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_modifier_value = {
					which = cavalry_power
					value = 0.05
				}
				NOT = {
					has_global_modifier_value = {
						which = cavalry_power
						value = 0.10
					}
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_1 
				duration = -1
			}
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_2 
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_3 
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_4 
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_5 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_modifier_value = {
					which = cavalry_power
					value = 0.10
				}
				NOT = {
					has_global_modifier_value = {
						which = cavalry_power
						value = 0.15
					}
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_2
				duration = -1
			}
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_1
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_3 
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_4 
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_5 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_modifier_value = {
					which = cavalry_power
					value = 0.15
				}
				NOT = {
					has_global_modifier_value = {
						which = cavalry_power
						value = 0.20
					}
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_3
				duration = -1
			}
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_1 
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_2 
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_4 
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_5 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_modifier_value = {
					which = cavalry_power
					value = 0.20
				}
				NOT = {
					has_global_modifier_value = {
						which = cavalry_power
						value = 0.25
					}
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_4
				duration = -1
			}
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_1
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_2 
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_3 
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_5 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_modifier_value = {
					which = cavalry_power
					value = 0.25
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_5
				duration = -1
			}
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_1 
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_2 
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_3 
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Elephant_Cavalry_4
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.183.a
		
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.184
	title = reform_me_events.184.t
	desc = reform_me_events.184.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_government_attribute = enables_siamese_honor
				OR = {
					AND = {
						legitimacy = 75
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = siamese_national_pride }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { legitimacy = 75 }
						has_country_modifier = siamese_national_pride
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = {	legitimacy = 50	}
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = siamese_national_shame }
					}
					AND = {
						legitimacy = 50
						has_country_modifier = siamese_national_shame
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_country_modifier = siamese_national_pride
					has_country_modifier = siamese_national_shame
				}
				NOT = { has_government_attribute = enables_siamese_honor }
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				legitimacy = 75
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = siamese_national_pride }
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = siamese_national_pride 
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { legitimacy = 75 }
				has_country_modifier = siamese_national_pride
			}
			remove_country_modifier = siamese_national_pride 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {	legitimacy = 50	}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = siamese_national_shame }
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = siamese_national_shame
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				legitimacy = 50
				has_country_modifier = siamese_national_shame
			}
			remove_country_modifier = siamese_national_shame 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_government_attribute = enables_siamese_honor }
			}
			remove_country_modifier = siamese_national_pride
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.184.a
		
	}
}

country_event = {

		OR = {
			AND = {

					all_subject_country = {
						NOT = {
							is_colonial_nation = yes
							is_subject_of_type = tributary_state
						}
						is_part_of_hre = yes
					}
					amount = 1
				}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = GE_Imperial_Circle_1 }
			}
			AND = {
				calc_true_if = {
					all_subject_country = {
						NOT = {
							is_colonial_nation = yes
							is_subject_of_type = tributary_state
						}
						is_part_of_hre = yes
					}
					amount = 2
				}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = GE_Imperial_Circle_2 }
			}
			AND = {
				calc_true_if = {
					all_subject_country = {
						NOT = {
							is_colonial_nation = yes
							is_subject_of_type = tributary_state
						}
						is_part_of_hre = yes
					}
					amount = 3
				}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = GE_Imperial_Circle_3 }
			}
			AND = {
				calc_true_if = {
					all_subject_country = {
						NOT = {
							is_colonial_nation = yes
							is_subject_of_type = tributary_state
						}
						is_part_of_hre = yes
					}
					amount = 4
				}

							is_colonial_nation = yes

						}

								is_colonial_nation = yes
								is_subject_of_type = tributary_state
							}
							is_part_of_hre = yes
						}
						amount = 2
					}
				}
			}

				name = GE_Imperial_Circle_1
				duration = -1
				hidden = yes
			}
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Imperial_Circle_2

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.202
	title = reform_me_events.202.t
	desc = reform_me_events.202.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	

	trigger = {
		has_government_attribute = enables_republican_guard
		OR = {
			AND = {
				republican_tradition = 60
				NOT = { republican_tradition = 70 }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = GE_Republican_Guard_1 }
			}
			AND = {
				republican_tradition = 70
				NOT = { republican_tradition = 80 }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = GE_Republican_Guard_2 }
			}
			AND = {
				republican_tradition = 80
				NOT = { republican_tradition = 90 }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = GE_Republican_Guard_3 }
			}
			AND = {
				republican_tradition = 90
				NOT = { republican_tradition = 100 }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = GE_Republican_Guard_4 }
			}
			AND = {
				republican_tradition = 100
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = GE_Republican_Guard_5 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}

			remove_country_modifier = GE_Republican_Guard_4
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Republican_Guard_5

			remove_country_modifier = GE_Republican_Guard_3
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Republican_Guard_4
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Republican_Guard_5
		}
		if = {

				republican_tradition = 80
				NOT = { republican_tradition = 90 }

			}

country_event = {
	id = reform_me_events.205
	title = reform_me_events.205.t
	desc = reform_me_events.205.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_government_attribute = enables_huaca_cults
				any_owned_province = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							OR = {
								has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
								has_owner_culture = yes
							}
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = GE_Huaca_Cults }
						}
						AND = {
							OR = {
								has_owner_accepted_culture = no
								has_owner_culture = no
							}
							has_province_modifier = GE_Huaca_Cults
						}
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { has_government_attribute = enables_huaca_cults }
				any_owned_province = {
					has_province_modifier = GE_Huaca_Cults
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	option = {
		name = reform_me_events.205.a
		
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = GE_Huaca_Cults }
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = GE_Huaca_Cults
				duration = -1
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_owner_accepted_culture = no
				}
				has_province_modifier = GE_Huaca_Cults
			}
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Huaca_Cults
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				owner = {NOT = { has_government_attribute = enables_huaca_cults }}
			}
			remove_country_modifier = GE_Huaca_Cults
		}
	}
}

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_government_attribute = enables_unified_drills }
			AND = {

				NOT = { num_of_subjects = 1 }
			}
		}
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = GE_Shared_Drills_1
			has_country_modifier = GE_Shared_Drills_2
			has_country_modifier = GE_Shared_Drills_3
			has_country_modifier = GE_Shared_Drills_4
			has_country_modifier = GE_Shared_Drills_5
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		remove_country_modifier = GE_Shared_Drills_1
		remove_country_modifier = GE_Shared_Drills_2
		remove_country_modifier = GE_Shared_Drills_3
		remove_country_modifier = GE_Shared_Drills_4
